<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  41.08;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -75.57;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 41.04;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -76.34;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(41.0600, -75.7500), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Hickory Run Truck Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>I-80 Exit 41 NW, White Haven, PA 18661</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-80 Exit 274 (PA 534)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(41.0600, -75.7700), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Bandit Truck Stop #2</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>I-80 Exit 41 (Rt 534), White Haven, PA 18661</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-80 Exit 41 (PA 534)</p>");
 });

var cTSE2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(41.0100, -76.2800), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE2);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE2, "click", function() {
     cTSE2.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Brennan's Auto/Truck Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>I-80 Exit 37, Mifflinville, PA 18631</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-80 Exit 37 (PA 339)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  41.57;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -87.12;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 41.57;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -87.50;

			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";

    function showMap() {

           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());

            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";

			map.addOverlay(term1);

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  39.97;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -74.91;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 39.69;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -75.51;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.6700, -75.4900), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>American Truck Stop - Carney's Point</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>414 Slapes Corner Rd, Carney's Point, NJ 08069</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-295 Exit 2 C (NJTP Exit 1)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.6900, -75.4500), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Flying J - Penns Grove</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>326 Slapes Corner Rd, Carney's Point, NJ 08069</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-295 Exit 2 C (NJ 140 W)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

</body>
</html>

    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  39.32;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -76.53;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 38.82;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -76.74;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.2800, -76.5500), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>TA #216 - Baltimore</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>5501 O'Donnell St Cutoff, Baltimore, MD 21224</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-95 Exit 57 (O'Donnell St) /I-895</p>");

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  37.94;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -77.47;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 37.67;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -77.45;

			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);

			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);

			map.addOverlay(term1);

			map.addOverlay(term2);

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  31.12;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -83.43;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 30.63;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -83.17;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(30.6453, -83.1869), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>TA #128 - Lake Park</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>6901 Belleville Rd, Lake Park, GA 31636</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-75 Exit 2 (Bellville Rd E)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(30.9913, -83.3887), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Sav-A-Ton #05</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>1311 Hwy 122 W, Hahira, GA 31632</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-75 Exit 29 (GA 122)</p>");
 });

var cTSE2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(31.1300, -83.4400), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE2);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE2, "click", function() {
     cTSE2.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Adel Truck Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>1503 W 4th St, Adel, GA 31620</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-75 Exit 39 (GA 37)</p>");
 });

var cTSE3 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(30.6400, -83.1900), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE3);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE3, "click", function() {
     cTSE3.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Flying J - Lake Park</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>7001 Lake Park-Bellville, Lake Park, GA 31636</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-75 Exit 2 (Bellville Rd W)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  42.24;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -71.59;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 41.98;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -72.18;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(42.0600, -72.1000), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Pilot #222 - Sturbridge</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>400 Rte 15 (Haynes St), Sturbridge, MA 01566</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-84 Exit 1 (MA 15)</p>");
 });

 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Flynn's Truck Stop</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>307 Hartford Tpke, Shrewsbury, MA 01545</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>US 20 and MA 140</p>");
 });

 map.addOverlay(cTSE2);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE2, "click", function() {
     cTSE2.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Westborough Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>I-90 (MATP) MM 105 WB, Westborough, MA 01581</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-90 (MATP) MM 105 WB</p>");

			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  35.36;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -78.55;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 35.13;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -78.75;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(35.2985, -78.5988), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Robin Hood Travel Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>I-95 Exit 77, Benson, NC 27501</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-95 Exit 77 (Hodges Chapel Rd)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(35.3171, -78.5761), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Sadler Travel Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>Jonesboro Rd, Exit 75, Dunn, NC 28335</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-95 Exit 75 (Jonesboro Rd)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1);

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  30.33;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -91.01;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 30.45;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -91.25;

			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2);

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  30.69;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -86.13;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 30.73;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -86.39;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(30.7200, -86.3500), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Lucky 13 Truck and Auto Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>328 Green Acres Rd, Mossy Head, FL 32433</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-10 Exit 13 (FL 285)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>

    function showMap() {

			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());

            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";

			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);

			map.addOverlay(term1);

    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  36.12;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -84.03;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 35.74;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -84.39;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2);

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  37.88;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -84.34;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 37.34;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -84.31;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(37.8200, -84.3200), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Clays Ferry Travel Center</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>120 Carr Lane, Richmond, KY 40475</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-75 Exit 97 (E to Service Rd)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(37.3606, -84.3368), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Derby City South Truck Plaza</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>1990 Richmond St, Mount Vernon, KY 40456</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-75 Exit 62 (US 25 N)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  31.56;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -97.12;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 31.09;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -97.39;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(31.1700, -97.3100), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>W-Wheels #3</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>6278 N General Bruce Rd, Temple, TX 76501</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-35 Exit 305 (Berger Rd)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(31.4500, -97.1700), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Pilot #432 - Robinson</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>8055 S I-35, Robinson, TX 76706</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-35 Exit 328 (Sun Valley Rd W)</p>");
 });

var cTSE2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(31.5000, -97.1400), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE2);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE2, "click", function() {
     cTSE2.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Flying J - Waco</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>2409 S New Rd, Waco, TX 76711</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-35 Exit 331 (New Rd)</p>");
 });

var cTSE3 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(31.1400, -97.3200), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE3);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE3, "click", function() {
     cTSE3.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Willie's 305 Truck Stop</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>6278 N. General Bruce Drive, Temple, TX 76501</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-35 Exit 305 (Berger Rd)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

</body>

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  44.39;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -123.06;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 44.11;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -123.04;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(44.1300, -123.0600), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>TA #078 - Eugene</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>32910 E Pearl St, Eugene, OR 97408</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-5E Exit 199</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

</body>

    function showMap() {

 var nTerminus2Lat = 40.72;

           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());

            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  41.74;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -106.84;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 41.76;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -107.50;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {

           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());

    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  36.27;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -86.74;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 36.03;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -86.78;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2);

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  39.74;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -86.14;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 39.37;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -85.94;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.5508, -86.0434), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Kiel Bros. Stop 95</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>3542 E 500 N, Whiteland, IN 46184</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-65 Exit 95 (Whiteland Rd)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.5500, -86.0357), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Flying J - Whiteland</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>4982 N 350 East, Whiteland, OH 46184</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-65 Exit 95 (Whiteland Rd)</p>");
 });

var cTSE2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.5500, -86.0400), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE2);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE2, "click", function() {
     cTSE2.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Pilot #037 - Whiteland</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>2962 County Road 500 North, Whiteland, IN 46184</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-65 Exit 95 (CR 500 N)</p>");
 });

var cTSE3 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.5500, -86.0400), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE3);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE3, "click", function() {
     cTSE3.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Pilot #397 - Whiteland</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>5115 North 300 East, Whiteland, IN 46184</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-65 Exit 95 (IN 500)</p>");
 });

var cTSE4 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(39.6100, -86.0700), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE4);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE4, "click", function() {
     cTSE4.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Road Ranger #226</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>1601 E Main, Greenwood, IN 46143</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-65 Exit 99</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng)));

          }

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  34.97;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -82.01;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 34.67;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -82.54;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(34.9100, -82.1200), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>TA #025 - Spartanburg</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>1402 E Main St, Duncan, SC 29334</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-85, Exit 63 (SC 290)</p>");
 });

var cTSE1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(34.7000, -82.5000), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE1);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE1, "click", function() {
     cTSE1.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Pilot #063 - Piedmont</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>110 Frontage Road, Piedmont, SC 29673</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-85 Exit 35 (Hwy 86)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  32.28;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -90.00;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 32.32;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -90.32;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

			map.addOverlay(term1);

    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  32.55;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -93.51;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 32.48;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -94.09;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 });

       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());

			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2);

    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {

 var nTerminus1Lng = -76.53;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 38.82;

        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());

            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function showMap() {
        if (GBrowserIsCompatible()) {
			var nTerminus1Lat =  36.54;
 var nTerminus1Lng = -78.18;
 var nTerminus2Lat = 36.37;
 var nTerminus2Lng = -78.36;

var fullMapLat = (nTerminus1Lat + nTerminus2Lat) / 2;
			var fullMapLng = (nTerminus1Lng + nTerminus2Lng) / 2;

		            var map = new GMap2(document.getElementById("map"));
           	map.addControl(new GLargeMapControl());
        	map.addControl(new GScaleControl());
       		map.addControl(new GMapTypeControl());
			map.setCenter(new GLatLng(fullMapLat, fullMapLng), 9);
            //map.setCenter(new GLatLng(41.06, -75.92), 10);

						var keyboard = new GKeyboardHandler(map);

						var yellowicon = new GIcon();
			yellowicon.image = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_yellow.png";
			yellowicon.shadow = "http://labs.google.com/ridefinder/images/mm_20_shadow.png";
			yellowicon.iconSize = new GSize(12, 20);
			yellowicon.shadowSize = new GSize(22, 20);
			yellowicon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(6, 20);
			yellowicon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(5, 1);
			yellowicon.infoShadowAnchor = new GPoint(10, 23);
			
			var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 


			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

var cTSE0 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(36.3900, -78.3300), yellowicon);
 map.addOverlay(cTSE0);
 GEvent.addListener(cTSE0, "click", function() {
     cTSE0.openInfoWindowHtml("<h4>Chex Truck Stop</h4><h5>Address</h5><p>250 Fleming Rd, Henderson, NC 27536</p><h5>Directions</h5><p>I-85 Exit 220 (Fleming Rd)</p>");
 });

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 var term1 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus1Lat, nTerminus1Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term1); 
			});

			//map.addOverlay(new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng))); 
			var term2 = new GMarker(new GLatLng(nTerminus2Lat, nTerminus2Lng));
			map.addOverlay(term2); 
			});
          }
        }
    //]]>
</script>
